# SECTION 9: BLOOD SERVICE (ҚОН ХИЗМАТИ)

## 9.1 BLOOD SERVICE OVERVIEW

### Blood Service Organizational Structure
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                          BLOOD SERVICE OVERVIEW                                  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    MAIN SERVICE COMPONENTS:

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  1. DONOR REGISTRATION (Донорларни рўйхатга олиш)                        │
    │     - Voluntary donor enrollment and certification                        │
    │     - Donor history and eligibility tracking                              │
    │     Forms: 120-122-х/ш, 124-х/ш                                          │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  2. BLOOD COLLECTION (Қон олиш)                                          │
    │     - Whole blood donation                                                │
    │     - Plasma/cytapheresis procedures                                      │
    │     - Commission and cadaveric blood                                      │
    │     Forms: 123-126-х/ш                                                    │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  3. BLOOD TYPING AND SEROLOGY (Қон гуруҳи ва серология)                   │
    │     - ABO/Rh typing                                                       │
    │     - Standard serum preparation                                          │
    │     Forms: 127-129-х/ш                                                    │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  4. INFECTIOUS DISEASE SCREENING (Юқумли касалликлар скрининги)          │
    │     - HIV testing (ELISA, Western Blot)                                   │
    │     - Hepatitis B/C screening                                             │
    │     - Syphilis testing                                                    │
    │     - Brucellosis testing                                                 │
    │     Forms: 130, 142-144-х/ш                                               │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  5. COMPONENT PREPARATION (Қон компонентлари тайёрлаш)                    │
    │     - Plasma separation and freezing                                      │
    │     - Cryoprecipitate preparation                                         │
    │     - Washed erythrocyte preparation                                      │
    │     - Quality control and sterility testing                               │
    │     Forms: 131-136-х/ш                                                    │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  6. STORAGE AND DISTRIBUTION (Сақлаш ва тарқатиш)                         │
    │     - Blood bank inventory management                                     │
    │     - Distribution to healthcare facilities                               │
    │     - Unsuitable component disposal                                       │
    │     Forms: 137-141-х/ш, 132-х/ш                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘


    BLOOD SERVICE WORKFLOW:
    ═══════════════════════

    DONOR → COLLECTION → TESTING → PROCESSING → STORAGE → DISTRIBUTION
        │          │          │          │          │           │
        ▼          ▼          ▼          ▼          ▼           ▼
    ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐
    │120-124 │ │123-126 │ │130,142-│ │133-136 │ │138,141 │ │137,139 │
    │ Donor  │ │ Blood  │ │  144   │ │Compon- │ │Reserve │ │ Distri-│
    │ Regist │ │Collect.│ │Testing │ │  ent   │ │Storage │ │ bution │
    └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘
```

## 9.2 DONOR REGISTRATION AND CERTIFICATION CLUSTER

### Donor Enrollment Workflow
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    DONOR REGISTRATION WORKFLOW                                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    POTENTIAL DONOR ARRIVES
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     121-х/ш         │     VOLUNTARY DONOR REGISTRATION JOURNAL
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Donor Registration │     Records:
    │  Journal            │     - Date of visit
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Donor name and demographics
              │                  - Contact information
              │                  - Initial eligibility screening
              │                  - Referral source
              │
              │ If donor qualifies for registration:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     122-х/ш         │     DONOR REGISTRATION CARD
    │  (Card, 50yr)       │
    │  Donor Account Card │     Contains:
    │                     │     - Permanent donor ID
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Complete demographic data
              │                  - Blood type (once determined)
              │                  - Medical history
              │                  - Donation history
              │                  - Deferral records
              │
              │ For voluntary (unpaid) donors:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     124-х/ш         │     VOLUNTARY DONOR CARD
    │  (Card, 50yr)       │
    │  Voluntary Donor    │     Contains:
    │  Card               │     - Donor ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Donation records
                                - Benefits/awards tracking
                                - Honor donor status

                                         │
                                         │ After donation:
                                         │
                                         ▼
                              ┌─────────────────────┐
                              │     120-х/ш         │
                              │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
                              │  Donor Certificate  │
                              │  Registration       │
                              │                     │
                              │  Tracks:            │
                              │  - Certificates     │
                              │    issued           │
                              │  - Certificate #    │
                              │  - Donation date    │
                              │  - Paid leave       │
                              │    documentation    │
                              └─────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Donor Registration:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 121-х/ш | 122-х/ш | Donor demographics, initial screening | New donor registered |
| 121-х/ш | 124-х/ш | Voluntary donor data | If unpaid donor |
| 122-х/ш | 124-х/ш | Donor ID, donation history | Donation completed |
| 122/124-х/ш | 120-х/ш | Certificate issued | Post-donation |

## 9.3 BLOOD COLLECTION CLUSTER

### Blood Collection Methods and Documentation
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    BLOOD COLLECTION WORKFLOW                                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    REGISTERED DONOR (from 122-х/ш)
              │
              │ Pre-donation screening (medical exam, hemoglobin check)
              │
              ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
              │                                                                 │
              ▼                                                                 ▼
    ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐                   ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐
    │        WHOLE BLOOD DONATION          │                   │     APHERESIS PROCEDURES             │
    │                                      │                   │                                      │
    │  Standard 450ml whole blood          │                   │  Selective component collection      │
    │  collection                          │                   │                                      │
    │                                      │                   │  ┌─────────────────────┐            │
    │  Records in:                         │                   │  │     123-х/ш         │            │
    │  - 122-х/ш (Donor card)              │                   │  │  (Journal, 25yr)    │            │
    │  - 124-х/ш (if voluntary)            │                   │  │  Plasma/Cytapheresis│            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  Component Journal  │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │                     │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  Records:           │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  - Procedure type   │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  - Volume collected │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  - Anticoagulant    │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  - Procedure time   │            │
    │                                      │                   │  │  - Donor reactions  │            │
    │                                      │                   │  └─────────────────────┘            │
    └───────────────────┬──────────────────┘                   └───────────────────┬────────────────┘
                        │                                                          │
                        └──────────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────┘
                                                   │
                                                   ▼
    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                              SPECIAL COLLECTION SCENARIOS                                      │
    ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
    │                                                                                               │
    │   COMMISSION COLLECTION                          CADAVERIC BLOOD                             │
    │   (With oversight committee)                     (From deceased donors)                      │
    │                                                                                               │
    │   ┌─────────────────────┐                        ┌─────────────────────┐                     │
    │   │     125-х/ш         │                        │     126-х/ш         │                     │
    │   │  (Journal, 25yr)    │                        │  (Journal, 25yr)    │                     │
    │   │  Commission Blood   │                        │  Cadaveric Blood    │                     │
    │   │  Collection Journal │                        │  Preparation Journal│                     │
    │   │                     │                        │                     │                     │
    │   │  Records:           │                        │  Records:           │                     │
    │   │  - Committee        │                        │  - Deceased ID      │                     │
    │   │    members          │                        │  - Time of death    │                     │
    │   │  - Donor consent    │                        │  - Collection time  │                     │
    │   │  - Collection date  │                        │  - Volume obtained  │                     │
    │   │  - Volume           │                        │  - Special testing  │                     │
    │   │  - Authorization    │                        │    requirements     │                     │
    │   └─────────────────────┘                        └─────────────────────┘                     │
    │                                                                                               │
    │   NOTE: Commission collection used for:          NOTE: Cadaveric blood requires:            │
    │   - Autologous donations                         - Extended testing protocols               │
    │   - Directed donations                           - Strict time limits                       │
    │   - Emergency collections                        - Special documentation                    │
    │                                                                                               │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

                                                   │
                                                   │ All collected blood →
                                                   │
                                                   ▼
                              ┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
                              │           TO TESTING CLUSTER            │
                              │                                         │
                              │  Blood samples sent for:               │
                              │  - ABO/Rh typing (129-х/ш)             │
                              │  - Infectious disease testing          │
                              │    (142-144-х/ш)                       │
                              │  - Clinical/biochemical tests          │
                              │    (144-х/ш)                           │
                              └─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Blood Collection:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 122-х/ш | 123-х/ш | Donor ID, blood type | Apheresis procedure |
| 122-х/ш | 125-х/ш | Donor data | Commission collection |
| 125-х/ш | 133-х/ш | Collection data | Component processing |
| 126-х/ш | 131-х/ш | Cadaveric blood ID | Sterility testing |
| 123-х/ш | 133-х/ш | Component data | Processing |

## 9.4 BLOOD TYPING AND SEROLOGY CLUSTER

### Blood Typing and Serum Preparation
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

    BLOOD SAMPLE FROM COLLECTION
              │

              │                  - Confirmation testing
              │
              │ Results recorded and sent to:
              │
              ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
              │                                                                 │
              ▼                                                                 ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐                               ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     122-х/ш         │                               │     124-х/ш         │
    │  Donor Card         │                               │  Voluntary Donor    │
    │                     │                               │  Card               │
    │  Updates:           │                               │                     │
    │  - Blood type       │                               │  Updates:           │
    │  - Rh factor        │                               │  - Blood type       │
    └─────────────────────┘                               └─────────────────────┘


    STANDARD SERUM PREPARATION:
    ═══════════════════════════

    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     127-х/ш         │     ABO SYSTEM STANDARD AND ANTI-Rh SERUM PREPARATION
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Serum Preparation  │     Records:
    │  Journal            │     - Incoming products for serum preparation
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Raw material source
              │                  - Processing date
              │                  - Batch numbers
              │
              │ Production of typing reagents:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     128-х/ш         │     ABO STANDARD AND ANTI-Rh SERUM REGISTRATION
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Prepared Serum     │     Records:
    │  Registration       │     - Serum type produced
    └─────────────────────┘     - Batch number
                                - Production date
                                - Expiration date
                                - Titer/potency
                                - Quality control results
                                - Distribution to labs

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  SERUM TYPES PRODUCED:                                                    │
    │                                                                           │
    │  - Anti-A serum (for detecting A antigen)                                │
    │  - Anti-B serum (for detecting B antigen)                                │
    │  - Anti-D (Rh) serum (for detecting Rh factor)                           │
    │  - Anti-human globulin (Coombs reagent)                                  │
    │                                                                           │
    │  Used for:                                                                │
    │  - Donor blood typing                                                     │
    │  - Pre-transfusion compatibility testing                                  │
    │  - Crossmatching at hospitals                                             │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Blood Typing:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 129-х/ш | 122-х/ш | Blood group, Rh factor | First-time donor |
| 129-х/ш | 124-х/ш | Blood group, Rh factor | Voluntary donor |
| 127-х/ш | 128-х/ш | Production batch data | Serum produced |
| 128-х/ш | 137-х/ш | Reagent distribution | Distribution |

## 9.5 INFECTIOUS DISEASE SCREENING CLUSTER

### Blood Safety Testing Workflow
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    INFECTIOUS DISEASE SCREENING                                  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    BLOOD SAMPLE FROM COLLECTION
              │
              │ Mandatory screening for all donations
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                          SCREENING PANEL                                     │
    │                                                                              │
    │   ┌─────────────────────┐                   ┌─────────────────────┐         │
    │   │     143-х/ш         │                   │     144-х/ш         │         │
    │   │  (Journal, 25yr)    │                   │  (Journal, 3yr)     │         │
    │   │  Syphilis, HCV,     │                   │  Clinical and       │         │
    │   │  HBsAg, HIV Tests   │                   │  Biochemical Tests  │         │
    │   │                     │                   │                     │         │
    │   │  INFECTIOUS PANEL:  │                   │  DONOR HEALTH:      │         │
    │   │  ┌─────────────────┐│                   │  ┌─────────────────┐│         │
    │   │  │ Syphilis (RPR)  ││                   │  │ Hemoglobin      ││         │
    │   │  │ HCV (anti-HCV)  ││                   │  │ Hematocrit      ││         │
    │   │  │ HBV (HBsAg)     ││                   │  │ ALT/AST         ││         │
    │   │  │ HIV (ELISA)     ││                   │  │ Total protein   ││         │
    │   │  └─────────────────┘│                   │  │ Bilirubin       ││         │
    │   │                     │                   │  └─────────────────┘│         │
    │   │  Records per donor: │                   │                     │         │
    │   │  - Donor ID         │                   │  Records:           │         │
    │   │  - Sample ID        │                   │  - Donor eligibility│         │
    │   │  - Test date        │                   │  - Health status    │         │
    │   │  - Results          │                   │  - Deferral reasons │         │
    │   │  - Reactive/Non     │                   │                     │         │
    │   └─────────────────────┘                   └─────────────────────┘         │
    │                                                                              │
    └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
              │
              │
    ┌─────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    ▼                                                                           ▼
NON-REACTIVE                                                              REACTIVE
(All tests negative)                                                      (Any positive)
    │                                                                           │
    │                                                                           │
    ▼                                                                           ▼
┌─────────────────┐                                            ┌─────────────────────┐
│  Blood cleared  │                                            │     142-х/ш         │
│  for processing │                                            │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
│                 │                                            │  HIV Seropositive   │
│  Proceeds to:   │                                            │  Donor Registration │
│  - Component    │                                            │  (ELISA & IB)       │
│    preparation  │                                            │                     │
│  - Storage      │                                            │  Records:           │
│  - Distribution │                                            │  - Donor ID         │
└─────────────────┘                                            │  - Initial ELISA    │
                                                               │  - Western Blot     │
                                                               │  - Confirmatory     │
                                                               │    results          │
                                                               │  - Notification     │
                                                               │    status           │
                                                               └──────────┬──────────┘
                                                                          │
                                                                          │ If HIV confirmed:
                                                                          │
                                                                          ▼
                                                               ┌─────────────────────┐
                                                               │   AIDS CENTER       │
                                                               │   (Section 8)       │
                                                               │                     │
                                                               │   Referral to:      │
                                                               │   - 181-х/ш         │
                                                               │     (Dispensary     │
                                                               │      Registration)  │
                                                               └─────────────────────┘


    BRUCELLOSIS SCREENING (Endemic areas):
    ═══════════════════════════════════════

    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     130-х/ш         │     BLOOD BRUCELLOSIS SEROLOGICAL TEST
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │     (Hendelsohn Reaction)
    │  Brucellosis        │
    │  Serological Test   │     Records:
    └─────────────────────┘     - Donor ID
                                - Test date
                                - Hendelsohn reaction result
                                - Titer if positive
                                - Action taken

    NOTE: Required in agricultural regions where brucellosis is endemic
```

### Relationship Details for Infectious Disease Screening:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 143-х/ш | 142-х/ш | HIV reactive result | Positive ELISA |
| 143-х/ш | 122-х/ш | Deferral status | Positive result |
| 142-х/ш | 181-х/ш (AIDS) | HIV+ donor notification | Confirmation |
| 144-х/ш | 122-х/ш | Health status | Abnormal results |
| 130-х/ш | 122-х/ш | Brucellosis status | If positive |
| 143-х/ш | 132-х/ш | Positive ID | Blood disposal |

## 9.6 COMPONENT PREPARATION AND QUALITY CONTROL CLUSTER

### Blood Component Manufacturing
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    COMPONENT PREPARATION WORKFLOW                                │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    CLEARED BLOOD FROM TESTING
              │
              │ Component separation and preparation
              │
    ┌─────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    ▼                              ▼                              ▼
┌─────────────────┐      ┌─────────────────┐      ┌─────────────────┐
│  PLASMA         │      │  CELLULAR       │      │  SPECIALIZED    │
│  PRODUCTS       │      │  PRODUCTS       │      │  PRODUCTS       │
└────────┬────────┘      └────────┬────────┘      └────────┬────────┘
         │                        │                        │
         ▼                        ▼                        ▼

    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     135-х/ш         │     PLASMA PREPARATION JOURNAL
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Plasma Preparation │     Types produced:
    │  Journal            │     - Fresh Frozen Plasma (FFP)
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Antistaphylococcal plasma
              │                  - Isoimmune plasma
              │
              │                  Records per batch:
              │                  - Source donation IDs
              │                  - Separation date
              │                  - Volume
              │                  - Freeze date/time
              │                  - Storage temperature
              │                  - Expiration date
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     134-х/ш         │     CRYOPRECIPITATE PREPARATION
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Cryoprecipitate    │     Records:
    │  Preparation        │     - Source plasma batch
    └─────────────────────┘     - Preparation date
                                - Factor VIII content
                                - Fibrinogen content
                                - Volume
                                - Expiration


    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     136-х/ш         │     WASHED ERYTHROCYTE PREPARATION
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Washed RBC         │     Records:
    │  Preparation        │     - Source unit ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Washing date
                                - Solution used
                                - Final hematocrit
                                - Leukocyte reduction status
                                - Expiration (24-hour shelf life)


    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     133-х/ш         │     VOLUNTARY DONOR BLOOD COMPONENT REGISTRATION
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Component          │     Master inventory:
    │  Inventory          │     - All components from voluntary donors
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Component type
              │                  - Donor source
              │                  - Volume
              │                  - ABO/Rh
              │                  - Processing date
              │                  - Status (available/reserved/issued)
              │
              │ Quality control:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     131-х/ш         │     PRESERVED BLOOD STERILITY TEST
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Sterility Testing  │     Records:
    │  Journal            │     - Unit/batch ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Sampling date
                                - Culture media used
                                - Incubation period
                                - Result (sterile/contaminated)
                                - Action if contaminated
                                         │
                                         │ If contaminated:
                                         │
                                         ▼
                              ┌─────────────────────┐
                              │     132-х/ш         │
                              │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
                              │  Unsuitable Blood   │
                              │  Component Disposal │
                              │                     │
                              │  Records:           │
                              │  - Unit ID          │
                              │  - Reason unsuitable│
                              │  - Disposal method  │
                              │  - Disposal date    │
                              │  - Witness signature│
                              └─────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Component Preparation:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 123-х/ш | 135-х/ш | Plasma collection data | Apheresis complete |
| 135-х/ш | 134-х/ш | Plasma batch ID | Cryo production |
| 133-х/ш | 136-х/ш | Source unit ID | Washed RBC prep |
| 133-х/ш | 131-х/ш | Sample for testing | QC sampling |
| 131-х/ш | 132-х/ш | Contaminated unit | Positive culture |
| 143-х/ш | 132-х/ш | Reactive unit | Positive serology |

## 9.7 STORAGE AND DISTRIBUTION CLUSTER

### Blood Product Distribution Workflow
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    STORAGE AND DISTRIBUTION WORKFLOW                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    PREPARED BLOOD COMPONENTS (from Component Preparation)
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     138-х/ш         │     BLOOD COMPONENT RESERVE DEPARTMENT RECEPTION
    │  (Journal, 25yr)    │
    │  Reserve Reception  │     Records:
    │  Journal            │     - Component type
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Unit/batch ID
              │                  - ABO/Rh
              │                  - Volume
              │                  - Received date
              │                  - Expiration date
              │                  - Storage location
              │                  - Temperature log
              │
              │ Storage in blood bank:
              │
              ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
              │                                                                 │
              ▼                                                                 ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐                               ┌─────────────────────┐
    │  WHOLE BLOOD &      │                               │  PLASMA PRODUCTS    │
    │  RBC COMPONENTS     │                               │                     │
    │                     │                               │  ┌─────────────────┐│
    │  Storage: 2-6°C     │                               │  │     141-х/ш     ││
    │  Shelf life varies  │                               │  │  (Journal, 3yr) ││
    │  by product         │                               │  │  Plasma         ││
    │                     │                               │  │  Reception      ││
    │                     │                               │  │  Journal        ││
    │                     │                               │  │                 ││
    │                     │                               │  │  Records:       ││
    │                     │                               │  │  - Plasma type  ││
    │                     │                               │  │  - Batch ID     ││
    │                     │                               │  │  - Volume       ││
    │                     │                               │  │  - Freeze date  ││
    │                     │                               │  └─────────────────┘│
    └─────────────────────┘                               └─────────────────────┘


    DISTRIBUTION PROCESS:
    ═════════════════════

    HEALTHCARE FACILITY REQUEST
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     139-х/ш         │     BLOOD COMPONENT AND PREPARATION REQUEST FORM
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │
    │  Request Form       │     Contains:
    │                     │     - Requesting facility
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Patient information (if known)
              │                  - Component type needed
              │                  - Quantity requested
              │                  - ABO/Rh requirements
              │                  - Urgency level
              │                  - Authorized signature
              │
              │ Request processed:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     137-х/ш         │     TREATMENT FACILITY BLOOD PRODUCT DISTRIBUTION
    │  (Journal, 25yr)    │
    │  Distribution       │     Records:
    │  Journal            │     - Request form reference
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Facility receiving
              │                  - Components issued:
              │                    - Unit ID
              │                    - Type
              │                    - ABO/Rh
              │                    - Volume
              │                    - Expiration
              │                  - Issue date/time
              │                  - Transport conditions
              │                  - Receiving signature
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     140-х/ш         │     BLOOD PREPARATION DISPATCH SUBMISSION
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Dispatch Journal   │     Records:
    │                     │     - Expedition/delivery ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Products sent
                                - Destination
                                - Departure time
                                - Transport personnel
                                - Delivery confirmation


    AT RECEIVING HOSPITAL:
    ══════════════════════

    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                             │
    │   Blood received at hospital links to:                                      │
    │                                                                             │
    │   ┌─────────────────┐           ┌─────────────────┐                        │
    │   │   009-х/ш       │           │   003-х/ш       │                        │
    │   │  Transfusion    │◄─────────►│  Inpatient Card │                        │
    │   │  Journal        │           │                 │                        │
    │   │  (Section 1)    │           │  Patient record │                        │
    │   └─────────────────┘           └─────────────────┘                        │
    │                                                                             │
    └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Storage and Distribution:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 133-х/ш | 138-х/ш | Component data | Storage intake |
| 135-х/ш | 141-х/ш | Plasma batch data | Plasma storage |
| 139-х/ш | 137-х/ш | Request details | Order processing |
| 137-х/ш | 140-х/ш | Dispatch items | Shipment prepared |
| 137-х/ш | 009-х/ш (Hospital) | Transfusion products | Products received |
| 138-х/ш | 132-х/ш | Expired units | Expiration reached |

## CROSS-SECTION LINKAGES: BLOOD SERVICE ↔ OTHER SECTIONS

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    BLOOD SERVICE CROSS-SECTION DATA FLOWS                        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    HOSPITAL (Section 1)                          BLOOD SERVICE (Section 9)
    ════════════════════                          ════════════════════════

    ┌─────────────────┐                          ┌─────────────────┐
    │    009-х/ш      │ ◄────────────────────────│    137-х/ш      │
    │  Transfusion    │     Blood products       │  Distribution   │
    │  Journal        │     delivered            │  Journal        │
```

# SECTION 10: SANITARY-EPIDEMIOLOGICAL SERVICE

## 10.1 SANITARY-EPIDEMIOLOGICAL SERVICE OVERVIEW

### SES Organizational Structure
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  SANITARY-EPIDEMIOLOGICAL SERVICE OVERVIEW                       │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    MAIN SERVICE COMPONENTS:

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  1. SANITARY SUPERVISION (Санитария назорати)                             │
    │     - Facility and construction oversight                                 │
    │     - Land allocation approvals                                           │
    │     - Project reviews and permits                                         │
    │     Forms: 145-152-х/ш                                                    │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  2. ENVIRONMENTAL SAMPLING (Аṭроф-муҳит намуналари)                       │
    │     - Water quality testing                                               │
    │     - Food safety analysis                                                │
    │     - Pesticide residue monitoring                                        │
    │     - Environmental swab collection                                        │
    │     Forms: 153-156-х/ш, 222-х/ш                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  3. INFECTIOUS DISEASE CONTROL (Юқумли касалликлар назорати)              │
    │     - Patient evacuation and isolation                                    │
    │     - Disinfection operations                                             │
    │     - Epidemiological investigation                                        │
    │     - Food poisoning response                                             │
    │     Forms: 157-164-х/ш, 214-х/ш                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  4. ZOONOTIC DISEASE SURVEILLANCE (Зооноз касалликлар)                    │
    │     - Brucellosis monitoring                                              │
    │     - Anthrax detection                                                   │
    │     - Other animal-transmitted diseases                                    │
    │     Forms: 165-171-х/ш, 196-197-х/ш, 202-203-х/ш                          │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  5. PARASITIC & VECTOR-BORNE DISEASES (Паразитар касалликлар)             │
    │     - Malaria surveillance                                                │
    │     - Leishmaniasis monitoring                                            │
    │     - Helminthiasis screening                                             │
    │     Forms: 168, 212, 230-х/ш                                              │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  6. LABORATORY STRAIN MANAGEMENT (Штаммлар бошқариш)                      │
    │     - Reference strain reception                                          │
    │     - Culture identification                                              │
    │     - International strain exchange                                        │
    │     Forms: 199-х/ш, 202-х/ш                                               │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  7. REGULATORY ACTIONS (Тартибга солиш)                                   │
    │     - Prohibition decisions                                               │
    │     - Examination protocols                                               │
    │     Forms: 221-х/ш, 224-х/ш                                               │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘


    SES WORKFLOW OVERVIEW:
    ══════════════════════

                            ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
                            │     SANITARY-EPIDEMIOLOGICAL        │
                            │           SERVICE (SES)              │
                            └─────────────────┬───────────────────┘
                                              │
             ┌────────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────┐
             │                                │                                │
             ▼                                ▼                                ▼
    ┌─────────────────┐            ┌─────────────────┐            ┌─────────────────┐
    │   PREVENTIVE    │            │   SURVEILLANCE   │            │   RESPONSE      │
    │   SUPERVISION   │            │   & MONITORING   │            │   ACTIVITIES    │
    │                 │            │                  │            │                 │
    │ - Facility      │            │ - Environmental  │            │ - Outbreak      │
    │   inspections   │            │   sampling       │            │   investigation │
    │ - Project       │            │ - Disease        │            │ - Disinfection  │
    │   approvals     │            │   surveillance   │            │ - Quarantine    │
    │ - Permits       │            │ - Lab testing    │            │ - Enforcement   │
    │                 │            │                  │            │                 │
```

## 10.2 SANITARY SUPERVISION OF FACILITIES CLUSTER

### Facility and Construction Oversight
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    SANITARY SUPERVISION WORKFLOW                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    NEW FACILITY OR CONSTRUCTION PROJECT
              │
              │ Land allocation request
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     146-х/ш         │     LAND ALLOCATION CONCLUSION
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │
    │  Land Allocation    │     Contains:
    │  Conclusion         │     - Site location description
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Environmental assessment
              │                  - Sanitary zone requirements
              │                  - Approval/rejection decision
              │
              │ Registered in:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     147-х/ш         │     LAND ALLOCATION CONCLUSIONS REGISTRATION
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Land Conclusions   │     Records:
    │  Registration       │     - Conclusion number
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Applicant
              │                  - Site location
              │                  - Decision date
              │                  - Approval status
              │
              │ If approved, project submitted:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     148-х/ш         │     PROJECT CONCLUSION
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │
    │  Project Sanitary   │     Contains:
    │  Conclusion         │     - Project specifications review
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Compliance with sanitary norms
              │                  - Water/sewage provisions
              │                  - Ventilation requirements
              │                  - Approval/modification needed
              │
              │ Registered in:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     149-х/ш         │     PROJECT CONCLUSIONS REGISTRATION
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Project Conclusions│     Records:
    │  Registration       │     - Project conclusion number
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Project name/type
              │                  - Location
              │                  - Decision
              │
              │ During construction:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     150-х/ш         │     CONSTRUCTION/REPAIR SANITARY SUPERVISION CARD
    │  (Card, 5yr)        │
    │  Construction       │     Contains:
    │  Supervision Card   │     - Construction site ID
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Inspection schedule
              │                  - Inspection findings
              │                  - Compliance issues
              │                  - Corrective actions required
              │                  - Final acceptance status
              │
              │ Upon completion, facility registered:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     145-х/ш         │     STATE SANITARY SUPERVISION OBJECTS REGISTRATION
    │  (Journal, 10yr)    │
    │  Supervised Objects │     MASTER REGISTRY of all facilities:
    │  Registry           │     - Object registration number
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Facility type/category
              │                  - Location
              │                  - Owner/operator
              │                  - Sanitary category
              │                  - Inspection schedule
              │
              │ Ongoing supervision:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     151-х/ш         │     CURRENT SANITARY SUPERVISION OBJECT CARD
    │  (Card, 10yr)       │
    │  Object Supervision │     Contains:
    │  Card               │     - Facility details
    └─────────────────────┘     - Inspection history
                                - Violations found
                                - Enforcement actions
                                - Compliance status


    SPECIAL: CHILDREN'S FACILITIES
    ═══════════════════════════════

    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     152-х/ш         │     CHILDREN'S RECREATION FACILITY SANITARY PERMIT
    │  (Blank, 1yr)       │
    │  Children's Camp    │     Seasonal permit for:
    │  Permit             │     - Summer camps
    └─────────────────────┘     - Recreation facilities
                                - Childcare centers
                                - Educational camps

                                Required before operation each season
```

### Relationship Details for Sanitary Supervision:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 146-х/ш | 147-х/ш | Land conclusion | Registration |
| 147-х/ш | 148-х/ш | Approved site | Project submission |
| 148-х/ш | 149-х/ш | Project conclusion | Registration |
| 149-х/ш | 150-х/ш | Approved project | Construction start |
| 150-х/ш | 145-х/ш | Completed facility | Final acceptance |
| 145-х/ш | 151-х/ш | Facility registration | Ongoing supervision |

## 10.3 ENVIRONMENTAL SAMPLING AND ANALYSIS CLUSTER

### Sampling Protocols and Testing
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ENVIRONMENTAL SAMPLING WORKFLOW                               │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    SAMPLING TRIGGERS:
    - Routine surveillance schedule
    - Complaint investigation
    - Outbreak response
    - Construction/permit requirements
              │
    ┌─────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    ▼                              ▼                              ▼
┌─────────────────┐      ┌─────────────────┐      ┌─────────────────┐
│  WATER SAMPLES  │      │  FOOD SAMPLES   │      │ ENVIRONMENTAL   │
│                 │      │                 │      │ SWABS           │
└────────┬────────┘      └────────┬────────┘      └────────┬────────┘
         │                        │                        │
         ▼                        ▼                        ▼

    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     153-х/ш         │     WATER SAMPLE COLLECTION PROTOCOL
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │
    │  Water Sample       │     Records:
    │  Collection         │     - Sample ID
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Collection date/time
              │                  - Source (tap, well, reservoir)
              │                  - Location
              │                  - Collection method
              │                  - Temperature at collection
              │                  - Transport conditions
              │
              │ Results recorded in:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     222-х/ш         │     DRINKING WATER TEST RESULTS
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Water Test Results │     Records:
    │  Journal            │     - Sample ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Chemical analysis (pH, hardness, nitrates)
                                - Bacteriological results (coliform, E.coli)
                                - Heavy metals
                                - Pass/fail determination
                                - Compliance status


    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     154-х/ш         │     FOOD PRODUCT SAMPLE COLLECTION PROTOCOL
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │
    │  Food Sample        │     Records:
    │  Collection         │     - Sample ID
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Food type/product name
              │                  - Manufacturer/source
              │                  - Collection location
              │                  - Production/expiration dates
              │                  - Storage conditions
              │                  - Reason for sampling
              │
              │ Tested for:
              │ - Microbiological contamination
              │ - Chemical contaminants
              │ - Aflatoxins
              │ - Pesticide residues
              │
              └────────────────────────────┐
                                           │
                                           ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐     ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     155-х/ш         │     │     162-х/ш         │
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │     │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Pesticide Residue  │     │  Food Poisoning     │
    │  Analysis Protocol  │     │  Case Registration  │
    │                     │     │                     │
    │  For agricultural   │     │  If contamination   │
    │  products           │     │  causes illness     │
    └─────────────────────┘     └─────────────────────┘


    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     156-х/ш         │     ENVIRONMENTAL SWAB COLLECTION PROTOCOL
    │  (Blank, 3yr)       │
    │  Environmental      │     Records:
    │  Swab Collection    │     - Swab ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Collection surface/object
                                - Location
                                - Date/time
                                - Collection technique
                                - Transport medium used

                                Used for:
                                - Equipment hygiene verification
                                - Food preparation surfaces
                                - Medical equipment
                                - Healthcare facilities


    WATER RESERVOIR MONITORING:
    ═══════════════════════════

    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     168-х/ш         │     WATER RESERVOIR CONDITION DESCRIPTION
    │  (Blank, 5yr)       │
    │  Water Reservoir    │     Contains:
    │  Assessment         │     - Reservoir identification
    └─────────────────────┘     - Physical condition
                                - Water quality parameters
                                - Surrounding land use
                                - Pollution sources
                                - Vector breeding potential
                                - Recommendations
```

### Relationship Details for Environmental Sampling:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|

| 154-х/ш | 162-х/ш | Food contamination | Illness reported |

| 156-х/ш | 160-х/ш | Contamination found | Disinfection needed |
| 168-х/ш | 153-х/ш | Reservoir risk | Water sampling |
| 168-х/ш | 212-х/ш | Vector breeding | Malaria surveillance |

## 10.4 INFECTIOUS DISEASE CONTROL CLUSTER

### Outbreak Response and Disinfection
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    INFECTIOUS DISEASE CONTROL WORKFLOW                           │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    INFECTIOUS DISEASE CASE IDENTIFIED
    (from healthcare facility via 058-х/ш Urgent Notification)
              │
              │ SES notified and responds
              │
    ┌─────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    ▼                                                                           ▼
PATIENT MANAGEMENT                                            EPIDEMIOLOGICAL
                                                              INVESTIGATION
    │                                                              │
    ▼                                                              ▼
┌─────────────────────┐                               ┌─────────────────────┐
│     157-х/ш         │                               │     161-х/ш         │
│  (Blank, 3yr)       │                               │  (Card, 5yr)        │
│  Infectious Patient │                               │  Epidemiological    │
│  Evacuation Form    │                               │  Investigation Card │
│                     │                               │                     │
│  Records:           │                               │  Contains:          │
│  - Patient ID       │                               │  - Case ID          │
│  - Disease          │                               │  - Index case data  │
│  - Transport type   │                               │  - Contact tracing  │
│  - Destination      │                               │  - Source of        │
│  - Precautions      │                               │    infection        │

          │                                           │  - Contributing     │
          │                                           │    factors          │
          │                                           │  - Recommendations  │
          │                                           └─────────────────────┘
          │
          │ Registered in:
          │
          ▼
┌─────────────────────┐
│     158-х/ш         │     INFECTIOUS PATIENT EVACUATION REGISTRATION
│  (Journal, 5yr)     │
│  Evacuation         │     Records:
│  Registration       │     - Evacuation ID
└─────────┬───────────┘     - Patient data
          │                  - Disease
          │                  - Transport details
          │                  - Receiving facility
          │
          │ At patient location/focus:
          │
          ▼

│                          DISINFECTION OPERATIONS                               │
├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                               │

│   │  Focus Disinfection │              │  Chamber Disinfection│               │
│   │  Registration       │              │  Journal            │               │
│   │                     │              │                     │               │
│   │  ENVIRONMENTAL:     │              │  MATERIAL:          │               │

│                          │  Results            │                             │
│                          │                     │                             │
│                          │  Quality control:   │                             │

└───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘


    FOOD POISONING RESPONSE:
    ════════════════════════

              │
              ▼

              │                  - Number affected
```

| 160-х/ш | 214-х/ш | Disinfectant used | QC verification |

## 10.5 ZOONOTIC DISEASE SURVEILLANCE - BRUCELLOSIS CLUSTER

### Brucellosis Detection and Monitoring
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    BRUCELLOSIS SURVEILLANCE WORKFLOW                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    BRUCELLOSIS SURVEILLANCE SOURCES:
    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
```

### Relationship Details for Brucellosis Surveillance:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 166-х/ш | 165-х/ш | Positive serology | Culture obtained |
| 167-х/ш | 165-х/ш | Positive product | Culture isolation |
| 165-х/ш | 196-х/ш | Isolate data | Case conclusion |
| 165-х/ш | 197-х/ш | Culture ID request | Identification |
| 130-х/ш (Blood) | 166-х/ш | Methodology coordination | Standardization |

## 10.6 ZOONOTIC DISEASE SURVEILLANCE - ANTHRAX CLUSTER

### Anthrax Detection and Response
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    ANTHRAX SURVEILLANCE WORKFLOW                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    ANTHRAX SURVEILLANCE SOURCES:
    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    │   HUMAN CASES              ENVIRONMENTAL            ANIMAL CASES         │
    │   (skin, inhalation,       (soil, water,           (sudden death in     │
    │    gastrointestinal)       contaminated areas)     livestock)           │
    │                                                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
              │                          │                          │
              │                          │                          │
              └──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┘
                                         │
                                         ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     169-х/ш         │     ANTHRAX TEST REGISTRATION JOURNAL
    │  (Journal, 10yr)    │
    │  Anthrax Testing    │     Records:
    │  (Environmental &   │     - Sample ID
    │   Patient samples)  │     - Source type
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Collection location
              │                  - Test method (microscopy, culture, PCR)
              │                  - Result
              │                  - Notification if positive
              │
              │ Biological confirmation:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     170-х/ш         │     BIOPROBE REGISTRATION JOURNAL
    │  (Journal, 10yr)    │
    │  Bioprobe Testing   │     Records:
    │  (Animal inoculation│     - Bioprobe ID
    │   for confirmation) │     - Sample tested
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Animal species used
              │                  - Inoculation date
              │                  - Observation period
              │                  - Outcome
              │                  - Pathological findings
              │
              │ If positive, isolate characterized:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     171-х/ш         │     ANTHRAX MICROBE CHARACTERISTICS
    │  (Blank, 10yr)      │
    │  Anthrax Strain     │     Contains:
    │  Description        │     - Strain ID
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Source and location
              │                  - Morphology
              │                  - Virulence factors
              │                  - Capsule presence
              │                  - Sensitivity testing
              │                  - Epidemiological significance
              │
              │ Strain received from external sources:
              │
    ┌─────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    ▼                                                                           ▼
┌─────────────────────┐                                      ┌─────────────────────┐
│     202-х/ш         │                                      │     203-х/ш         │
│  (Blank, 5yr)       │                                      │  (Journal, 10yr)    │
│  Strain Reception   │                                      │  Anthrax Strain     │
│  Protocol           │                                      │  Identification     │
│                     │                                      │  Results            │
│  Records:           │                                      │                     │
│  - Strain ID        │                                      │  Records:           │
│  - Source lab       │                                      │  - Identification   │
│  - Receipt date     │                                      │    method           │
│  - Transport        │                                      │  - Molecular typing │
│    conditions       │                                      │  - Genetic markers  │
│  - Verification     │                                      │  - Comparison to    │
│  - Storage          │                                      │    reference strains│
│                     │                                      │  - Final            │
│                     │                                      │    identification   │
└─────────────────────┘                                      └─────────────────────┘


    EMERGENCY RESPONSE:
    ════════════════════

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    │   Positive anthrax detection triggers:                                   │
    │                                                                           │
    │   1. Immediate notification to health authorities (058-х/ш linkage)     │
    │   2. Environmental disinfection (160-х/ш)                               │
    │   3. Contact tracing and prophylaxis                                     │
    │   4. Animal carcass disposal protocols                                   │
    │   5. Quarantine zone establishment                                       │
    │   6. Prohibition orders if needed (221-х/ш)                             │
    │                                                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Anthrax Surveillance:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 169-х/ш | 170-х/ш | Positive sample | Bioprobe confirmation |
| 170-х/ш | 171-х/ш | Confirmed isolate | Characterization |
| 202-х/ш | 203-х/ш | External strain | Identification |
| 169-х/ш | 160-х/ш | Contamination site | Disinfection |
| 171-х/ш | 221-х/ш | Confirmed case | Prohibition order |

## 10.7 PARASITIC AND VECTOR-BORNE DISEASES CLUSTER

### Special Surveillance Programs
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    PARASITIC & VECTOR-BORNE DISEASE SURVEILLANCE                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

    MALARIA AND TICK-BORNE DISEASES:
    ═════════════════════════════════

    SUSPECTED CASE (fever, travel history, tick bite)
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     212-х/ш         │     MALARIA AND TICK-BORNE TYPHUS BLOOD TEST
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Malaria/Typhus     │     Records:
    │  Testing            │     - Patient ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Sample date
                                - Travel history
                                - Tick exposure history
                                - Blood smear results
                                  - Plasmodium species
                                  - Parasitemia level
                                - Typhus serology
                                  - Rickettsia antibodies
                                  - Titer levels
                                - Treatment initiated

                                Linked to:
                                - 168-х/ш (water reservoir - breeding sites)
                                - Vector control programs


    LEISHMANIASIS SURVEILLANCE:
    ════════════════════════════

    SUSPECTED CASE (skin lesions, visceral symptoms)
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     230-х/ш         │     LEISHMANIASIS EXAMINATION REGISTRATION
    │  (Journal, 5yr)     │
    │  Leishmaniasis      │     Records:
    │  Testing            │     - Patient ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Lesion description
                                - Geographic exposure
                                - Microscopy results
                                  - Amastigotes in tissue
                                - Culture results
                                - Species identification
                                - Treatment tracking

                                Linked to:
                                - Vector control (sandfly)
                                - Geographic mapping
                                - Endemic area surveillance


    HELMINTHIASIS AND INTESTINAL PROTOZOA:
    ═══════════════════════════════════════

    SCREENING POPULATION (food handlers, children, at-risk groups)
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     164-х/ш         │     HELMINTHIASIS AND INTESTINAL PROTOZOA EXAMINATION
    │  (Journal, 3yr)     │
    │  Parasitology       │     Records:
    │  Screening          │     - Patient/subject ID
    └─────────────────────┘     - Sample type (stool)
                                - Collection date
                                - Examination method
                                  - Direct microscopy
                                  - Concentration techniques
                                  - Scotch tape test
                                - Findings:
                                  - Helminth eggs/larvae
                                  - Protozoan cysts/trophozoites
                                - Species identified
                                - Treatment referred

                                Used for:
                                - Food handler health certificates
                                - School health screening
                                - Outbreak investigation
                                - Environmental contamination assessment


    VECTOR-BORNE DISEASE ECOSYSTEM SURVEILLANCE:
    ═════════════════════════════════════════════

                              ┌─────────────────────┐
                              │     168-х/ш         │
                              │  Water Reservoir    │
                              │  Condition          │
                              │  Description        │
                              └──────────┬──────────┘
                                         │
                                         │ Identifies breeding habitats for:
                                         │
              ┌──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┐
              │                          │                          │
              ▼                          ▼                          ▼
    ┌─────────────────┐      ┌─────────────────┐      ┌─────────────────┐
    │    MOSQUITOES   │      │    SANDFLIES    │      │    TICKS        │
    │                 │      │                 │      │                 │
    │  → Malaria      │      │  → Leishmaniasis│      │  → Tick-borne   │
    │  → Dengue       │      │                 │      │    typhus       │
    │                 │      │                 │      │  → CCHF         │
    │                 │      │                 │      │  → Lyme disease │
    └─────────────────┘      └─────────────────┘      └─────────────────┘
              │                          │                          │
              └──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┘
                                         │
                                         ▼
                              ┌─────────────────────┐
                              │   VECTOR CONTROL    │
                              │   INTERVENTIONS     │
                              │                     │
                              │  - Larval control   │
                              │  - Adult control    │
                              │  - Habitat          │
                              │    modification     │
                              │  - Personal         │
                              │    protection       │
                              └─────────────────────┘
```

### Relationship Details for Parasitic/Vector-Borne Diseases:

| Source Form | Target Form | Data Transferred | Trigger |
|-------------|-------------|------------------|---------|
| 212-х/ш | 161-х/ш | Confirmed malaria | Epidemiological investigation |
| 230-х/ш | 161-х/ш | Confirmed leishmaniasis | Investigation |
| 168-х/ш | 212-х/ш | Breeding site risk | Enhanced surveillance |
| 164-х/ш | 160-х/ш | Environmental contamination | Disinfection |
| 164-х/ш | 154-х/ш | Food handler positive | Food sampling |

```
    └─────────────────────┘                             └─────────────────────┘


    STRAIN MANAGEMENT WORKFLOW:
    ═══════════════════════════

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    │   RECEPTION          VERIFICATION          STORAGE          DISTRIBUTION │
    │   (199, 202)         (197, 203)           (inventory)       (to labs)    │
    │       │                  │                    │                 │         │
    │       ▼                  ▼                    ▼                 ▼         │
    │   ┌────────┐        ┌────────┐          ┌────────┐        ┌────────┐    │
    │   │Import  │───────►│Identify│─────────►│Catalog │───────►│Issue   │    │
    │   │Check   │        │& Verify│          │& Store │        │Control │    │
    │   └────────┘        └────────┘          └────────┘        └────────┘    │
    │                                                                           │
    │   Biosafety requirements at each step:                                   │
    │   - Containment level verification                                       │
    │   - Chain of custody documentation                                       │
    │   - Access control logging                                               │
    │                                                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## 10.9 REGULATORY AND ADMINISTRATIVE CLUSTER

### Enforcement and Documentation
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     224-х/ш         │     SANITARY-EPIDEMIOLOGICAL EXAMINATION PROTOCOL

    │  Protocol           │     - Examination date
    └─────────┬───────────┘     - Object/facility inspected
              │                  - Persons present
              │                  - Areas examined
              │                  - Samples collected
              │                  - Findings
              │                  - Violations identified
              │                  - Recommendations
              │
              │ If violations require enforcement:
              │
              ▼
    ┌─────────────────────┐
    │     221-х/ш         │     PROHIBITION DECISION
    │  (Blank, 5yr)       │
    │  Prohibition        │     Contains:
    │  Order              │     - Decision number
    └─────────────────────┘     - Violating entity
                                - Nature of violation
                                - Prohibited activity
                                - Effective date
                                - Duration
                                - Conditions for lifting
                                - Appeal information
                                - Authorized signature

                                Types of prohibitions:
                                - Product seizure/destruction
                                - Facility closure
                                - Activity suspension
                                - Sales ban
                                - Import/export restriction


    PROHIBITION TRIGGERS:
    ═════════════════════

    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                                                                           │
    │   From Supervision:         From Surveillance:        From Outbreak:     │
    │   - 150/151-х/ш             - 162-х/ш (Food           - 161-х/ш          │
    │     (Facility violations)     poisoning)                (Epidemic focus) │
    │   - 224-х/ш                 - 169-171-х/ш             - 163-х/ш          │
    │     (Inspection findings)     (Anthrax detection)       (Urgent report)  │
    │   - 153-156-х/ш             - 166-167-х/ш                                │
    │     (Failed samples)          (Brucellosis)                              │
    │                                                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```
